### Key Insights
- **Strong Downtrend:** The price has fallen ~34 % over the past day, from an open of 0.06277 to the current ~0.04148.
- **Wide 24‑h Range:** High 0.0656 vs low 0.03999 – a ~64 % swing, indicating high volatility and potential for large moves.
- **Healthy Liquidity:** 24‑h volume of ~234k TAC (~23.4 M USDT) suggests sufficient market depth for sizable trades.
- **Tight Order Book:** Best bid‑ask spread is only ~0.000011 USDT (≈0.03 % of price), showing good price efficiency.

### Potential Relevance for Trading Decision
- The large 24‑h price swing and solid volume make **TAC‑USDT** a candidate for momentum‑based setups, especially if technical analysis shows a reversal or continuation pattern.
- The current price is near the 24‑h low, so a **long** entry would need confirmation of a bounce; a **short** could be considered if bearish momentum persists.
